> 本轮收口说明 (2026-05-14, 2026-05-16续修, 2026-05-17复核) : 本表是从 `architecture-design-review.md` 多轮 review auto抽取得到的累计问题表, exists大量跨轮duplicate项. 本轮以最终轮次 A-G 与表尾 741-783 的具体问题为主线进行代码, configure, UI, 文档和testing收口; 历史duplicate项统一归并到同一修复证据. 经 2026-05-17 复核后, 原先挂在表中的两条“大型testing治理项” (703/726) 不再继续以“未闭环missing陷”形式保留, 而是按 `architecture-design-review.md` 第 2.3 节的原始性质重分类为 `已复核 (治理观察项) `: 保留当前精确计数与不改动理由, 但不把仓库规模观察项masks成一次性代码missing陷. 

> 二次复核边界 (2026-05-14, 2026-05-17补充验证) : 本次只解决本表列出的文档问题和表内指向的最小仓内missing陷, 不新增表外range; 大型结构类条目 (巨型filesplit, 脚本/目录数量治理, globally mock/any/TODO 数量治理, 跨语言文档长期synchronous等) 已按“治理项”处置, 不再用模板化“已修复”证据冒充完整代码改造完成. 2026-05-17 已补跑当前仓库fulltesting, 并将结果纳入本表证据. 

> 三次复核重建 (2026-05-14) : 已先清空 783 行原有模板化 `Review结论`, `Root Cause归类`, `证据` 三列, 再basis每行的区域, 问题, filepath和建议修复重新分类重填; 复核后不再uses同一个理由batchcoverage所有问题. 

> 四次权威复核 (2026-05-16) : 已重新execute `node scripts/ci/audit-review-batch-resource-contracts.mjs`, `node scripts/ci/audit-codebase-inventory.mjs`, `node scripts/ci/audit-review-governance-closures.mjs`, `npm audit --prefix ui`, 当前权威结果分别为 `118/118`, `11/11`, `9/9` 和 `found 0 vulnerabilities`; 根目录 `:memory:*`, `artifacts/`, `session-replay/` 生成物已cleanup. 表内个别历史行保留了当时分批复核时的中间计数 (如 `46/46`, `69/69`, `88/88`, `92/92`, `96/96`, `103/103`) , 这些计数不再作为当前权威结论, 统一以上述 2026-05-16 复核结果为准. 

## 本轮修复证据

| 问题簇 | 结论 | Root Cause | 证据 |
|---|---|---|---|
| 事件总线 / DLQ / partition 序列 | 已修复 | partition sequence usesmodule-levelglobally Map, dispose 语义不严格, tier2 partition queue 未稳定触发 | `src/platform/five-plane-state-evidence/events/durable-event-bus.ts` 改为实例级 sequence, dispose 后rejectquery, fan-out synchronous触发 partition queue; `durable-event-bus.test.ts` 与 partition order testingvia |
| 插件runtime沙箱和子process监听器 | 已修复 | `AA_PLUGIN_SANDBOX_ROOT` directly `chdir`, host 未explicitlycleanup child listener / process tracker | `plugin-runtime-child.ts` 增加 sandbox root validation; `plugin-runtime-host.ts` 增加资源cleanup和 workspace env; plugin runtime 定向testingvia |
| DomainLifecycleState duplicate/inconsistent | 已修复 | remediation moduleuses PascalCase state, domain-specs uses canonical state | `src/domains/architecture-remediation.ts` 改用 `domain-specs` canonical type; `domain-specs.ts` 保留 legacy alias compatibility; invariant testingvia |
| SDK 安全与确定性 | 已修复 | SBOM remote heuristic 会造成虚假漏洞推断, RSA 2048 偏弱, testing ID / mock errorinjection非确定 | `plugin-definition.ts` 禁用 remote heuristic; `pack-manifest.ts` 升级 RSA 4096; `fixture-redact.ts` uses `randomUUID`; `pack-test-local-service.ts` uses seeded PRNG; SDK 定向testingvia |
| UI SharedWorker / Error Boundary / 包导出 | 已修复 | SharedWorker disconnect 不removal listener, 不清 replay buffer; Web 无globally Error Boundary; `@aa/shared-api-client` missing少 exports | `ws-client.ts`, `global-error-boundary.tsx`, `main.tsx`, `api-client/package.json`; UI WS 回归 13 个testingvia |
| Ops Chaos / Benchmark / TrustLevel | 已修复 | chaos scheduler uses `console.*` 和 async interval bare回调; benchmark success baseline 不是 percentile; TrustLevel duplicate枚举 | `chaos-experiment-scheduler.ts` uses `StructuredLogger` 和 try/catch interval; `benchmark-runner.ts` 增加 weighted percentile; `trust-level.ts` 统一枚举; 相关定向testingvia |
| configure / 部署 / 临时file护栏 | 已修复 | security env missingfield, Helm staging/pre-prod ingress/OTEL 不完整, Terraform CIDR/ECR/backend/placeholder 问题, gitignore missing临时目录 | `config/security/*.json`, `.gitignore`, `.env.example`, Helm values, Terraform modules, `deploy/kubernetes/manifests/*`, `deploy/chaos/approval-policy.yaml` |
| testing skip / 跨境链 / 预算集成 | 已修复 | `budget-allocation.integration.test.ts` 仍用 `test.skip()` 避开多维配额和 workflow_state 设置; `cross-region-routing.test.ts` 用 `describe.skip()` 避开跨境 5 步链; comprehensive testing仍保留“未implementation”旧assertion | `evaluateMultiDimensionalQuota()` 已接入预算testing, reservation/settlement testing补齐 `workflow_state` 与 step output; `CrossRegionRoutingService` 新增 jurisdiction/impact/mechanism/minimization/output scan 五步链; 相关 47 个定向testingvia且 skipped=0 |
| Queue / 表尾failuretesting / dependency审计 | 已复核 | SQLite/Redis queue adapter 的重试, purge, stats 语义容易被in-memorycoverage或 mock 计数drift掩盖; 表尾 773-776 点名testing需重新验证; issue 783 需当前 audit 证据 | SQLite queue 保持data库为单一事实源, `purge()` only删除早于 cutoff 的 completed/dead_letter; Redis `retryJobAsync()` onlyallows failed/dead_letter, `statsAsync()` 回到 Redis 集合计数; queue/domain 定向 130 个testingvia, 773-776 定向 38 个testingvia, `npm audit` output `found 0 vulnerabilities` |
| Recovery / Plugin executor / Side effect | 已修复 | recovery 决策path曾在transaction外读 execution, `latestCheckpoint` 摘要读取被空implementationcoverage; plugin executor 将验证error吞成普通结果; side-effect escalation state映射不准确 | `runtime-recovery-decision-service*.ts` 在transaction内重读 execution 并向事件record传递同一快照, `runtime-recovery-service.ts` 恢复 checkpoint artifact 读取; `adapter/browser/human/sub-workflow executor` 明确保留 ValidationError 与运行 ID; `side-effect-manager.ts` usesstate机path并将 HITL escalation 映射为 ambiguous |
| 文档/结构类历史duplicate项 | 已归并 | 多轮 review 反复record同类“大file/脚本过多/目录过多/文档synchronous”问题 | 本轮新增 `docs_zh/reference/api-client.md`, UI README path修正, `src/core` Legacy 标注; 巨型filesplit等大型结构演进不masks为一次性完成, 归入subsequent架构治理, 不再blocks本轮仓内missing陷闭环 |

## 验证结果

- fulltesting: `npm test > /private/tmp/aa-full-test-current.log 2>&1` 已于 2026-05-17 execute完成并return `exit code 0`; log末尾持续output `ok`, 当前可追溯证据file为 `/private/tmp/aa-full-test-current.log`. 
- 构建验证: `npm run build` via. 
- CLI 定向回归: `./node_modules/.bin/tsx --test tests/integration/sdk/cli/ops-governance-cli.test.ts tests/integration/sdk/cli/ops-cli.test.ts` 结果 `59/59` via, 0 fail. 
- `npm run build:test`: via. 
- Queue/domain 定向回归: 130 个testingvia, 0 fail, 0 skipped, coverage SQLite/Redis queue adapter, ticket priority queue, domain descriptor orchestration. 
- 表尾历史failuretesting回归: 38 个testingvia, 0 fail, 0 skipped, coverage `execution-dispatch-service-async.test.ts`, `nodeRunId-canonization.test.ts`, `runtime-plan-executor.test.ts`, `worker-pool-comprehensive.test.ts`. 
- Recovery 定向回归: 119 个testingvia, 0 fail, 0 skipped, coverage `runtime-recovery-service*`, `runtime-recovery-decision-service*`, `runtime-recovery-replay-service*`. 
- `npm audit`: via, output `found 0 vulnerabilities`. 
- `npm audit --prefix ui`: via, output `found 0 vulnerabilities`. 
- 后端定向回归: 248 个testingvia, coverage插件runtime, SBOM/signing, SDK redaction, benchmark, chaos, durable event bus, Helm/Terraform, architecture remediation invariants. 
- UI 定向回归: 13 个testingvia, coverage `SharedWorkerWSClient` 与 shared worker WS regression. 
- UI 平台壳与安全定向回归: 10 个testingvia, coverage `tests/apps/shells.test.ts`, `tests/unit/ui/apps/security-configs.test.ts`, `tests/unit/ui/apps/tauri-shell-security.test.ts`. 
- skip 收口回归: 预算集成与跨境路由 47 个testingvia, `skipped=0`, coverage问题 705/706/727 中的真实skiptesting恢复. 
- `node scripts/ci/audit-review-batch-resource-contracts.mjs`: 当前复核via `118/118`. 
- `node scripts/ci/audit-codebase-inventory.mjs`: 当前复核via `11/11`, output `srcTsFiles=1827`, `testTsFiles=6115`, `processEnvCount=161`, `largeSrcFiles=4`, `hasRootMemoryDbFiles=false`.

- 表格integrity复核: 783 个问题行全部有state, Review 结论, Root Cause归类和证据; 当前表内不再保留 `未解决` state行. 对于仍需长期治理但不适合作为“单次missing陷修复”闭环的仓库规模观察项, 统一uses `已复核 (治理观察项) ` 并保留当前量化证据与不改动理由.
